SQL>

SQL> 
SQL> 
SQL>

SQL>

SQL> 
SQL> REM a -> 97 , b -> 98 .. z -> 122
SQL>

SQL> 
SQL>

SQL> REM MULTI ROW COMPARISON OPERATORS :
SQL> 
SQL> REM MULTI ROW COMPARISON OPERATORS : FOR COMPARING MULTIPLE VALUES WITHIN SINGLE CONDITION.
SQL> 
SQL> REM LIST OF MULTI ROW COMPARISON OPERATORS : ANY/SOME  ALL
SQL> 
SQL> REM MULTI ROW OPERATORS DO NOT WORK ON IT'S OWN
SQL> 
SQL> REM MULTI ROW OPEARTORS ARE ALWAYS USED WITH SINGLE ROW OPERATORS
SQL> 
SQL> REM SYNTAX : OPERAND1 SINGLE ROW MULTI ROW (LIST OF OPERANDS COMMA SEPARATED)
SQL> 
SQL> REM EXAMPLE : DEPARTMENT_ID = ANY (20,60,110)
SQL> 
SQL> REM DEPARTMENT_ID : IS OPERAND 1
SQL> 
SQL> REM = : SINGLE ROW
SQL> 
SQL> REM ANY : MULTI ROW
SQL> 
SQL> REM (20,60,110) : (LIST OF OPERANDS COMMA SEPARATED)
SQL> 
SQL> 
SQL> REM EXAMPLE : DEPARTMENT_ID = ANY (20,60,110)
SQL> 
SQL> REM EXAMPLE : DEPARTMENT_ID = SOME (20,60,110)
SQL> 
SQL> 
SQL> REM = < > <= >= <>
SQL> 
SQL> 
SQL> REM = ANY    = SOME
SQL> 
SQL> REM <> ALL
SQL> 
SQL> 
SQL> 
SQL>

SQL> REM LOGICAL OPERATORS : () NOT AND OR
SQL> 
SQL> REM LOGICAL OPERATORS : () -NOT AND OR
SQL> 
SQL> REM LOGICAL OPERATORS : () -> NOT -> AND -> OR
SQL>  
SQL> REM NOT : IS PLACED JUST BEFORE CONDITION(S)
SQL> 
SQL> REM CONDITION : OPERAND1 OPERATOR OPERAND2
SQL> 
SQL> REM NOT : WILL REVERSE THE OUTPUT/OUTCOME/RESULT OF FOLLOWING CONDITION(S)
SQL> 
SQL> REM AND & OR : ARE PLACED BETWEEN TWO CONDITIONS, IT IS USED TO JOIN TWO CONDITIONS.
SQL> 
SQL> REM AND : IS USED WHEN WE WANT TO PROCESS ROWS WHICH SATISFIES BOTH CONDITIONS
SQL> 
SQL> REM OR : IS USED WHEN WE WANT TO PROCESS ROWS WHICH SATISFIES ATLEAST ONE CONDITION
SQL> 
SQL> SELECT * FROM EXAM;

       RNO    ENGLISH      MATHS                                                                                                                                                                        
---------- ---------- ----------                                                                                                                                                                        
         1         30         33
